You can also use the executive lounge and open the night windows at night. It was a bit hot when the heating was turned on. A circulating fan was delivered in the middle of the night, as well as cute little nail clippers and a panda doll. Seeing that I drank capsule coffee, he was very considerate and added more capsules. It was really, really worth it. By the way, the executive lounge has a nice view and the food is pretty good.
Finally, the hotel's location is excellent. It only takes 15 minutes by bicycle to reach Tianfu Square, People's Park, Kuanzhai Alley, and Wuhou Temple Jinli. It's really great! The subway entrance is just outside the hotel and turn left.
Next time I come, stay at Jinjiang Hotel.

The executive room can go to the VIP building, and go to the executive corridor on the 27th floor to enjoy breakfast, afternoon tea, and various pastries. Moreover, the swimming pool on the VIP building is separate from this side. The ordinary rooms here can only swim in this side, that is, the east building of Jin Jiang Hotel, and cannot go to the VIP building.
In other words, the east building of Jinjiang Hotel is the room I booked. It has a swimming pool on the second floor. The swimming pool is 22 meters long. The water quality is relatively clear, the service is relatively good, and the feeling of swimming is very good, and the top is made of glass. You can bask in the sun and swim. Looking at this room at around 500 yuan, the price/performance ratio is still super high.

Well, on the whole, the quality of service staff in the hotel is relatively good, indeed the quality of a five-star hotel.

Spend about 500 yuan to enjoy five-five-star service, and it feels really good, but the facilities in the room are a bit outdated.
